==========================The_first_checker_query=========================
You are an expert in writing java rule checkers and I need your help to generate a custom java rule checker in PMD tool version 7.0.0. 
I will give you a rule description, which may contain multiple violations. You just need to generate a checker that can check the violations of the given test case.

The following is a description of the rule and the corresponding counterexample test case and the AST of the counterexample test case:

Rule description: The null check is broken since it will throw a NullPointerException itself. It is likely that you used || instead of && or vice versa.;
The test case corresponding to the rule:
```
// should be &&
public class Foo {
    Object buz;
    Object bar(Object list) {
        if (list != null || !list.equals(buz)) {
            return list;
        }
    }
}
The description of this test case is: bad 1
The number of violating the rule in this test case is: 1

```

==========5轮中每一轮为第一个测试用例生成的checker===============
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.errorprone;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class BrokenNullCheckRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public BrokenNullCheckRule() {
        super(ASTIfStatement.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTIfStatement node, Object data) {
        ASTInfixExpression infixExpression = node.getFirstChildOfType(ASTInfixExpression.class);
        if (infixExpression != null) {
            boolean hasNullCheck = infixExpression.getFirstChildOfType(ASTNullLiteral.class) != null;
            boolean hasMethodCall = infixExpression.getFirstChildOfType(ASTMethodCall.class) != null;
            if (hasNullCheck && hasMethodCall) {
                boolean isOrExpression = infixExpression.getImage().equals("||");
                if (isOrExpression) {
                    addViolation(data, node);
                }
            }
        }

        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

==========5轮中每一轮为第一个测试用例生成的checker===============
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.errorprone;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class BrokenNullCheckRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public BrokenNullCheckRule() {
        super(ASTIfStatement.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTIfStatement node, Object data) {
        if(node.jjtGetNumChildren() > 0) {
            if(node.jjtGetChild(0) instanceof ASTInfixExpression) {
                ASTInfixExpression expr = (ASTInfixExpression) node.jjtGetChild(0);
                if(expr.getImage().equals("||")) { // check for || operator
                    if(expr.jjtGetChild(0) instanceof ASTInfixExpression) {
                        ASTInfixExpression leftExpr = (ASTInfixExpression) expr.jjtGetChild(0);
                        if(leftExpr.jjtGetChild(0) instanceof ASTNullLiteral) { // check for null check
                            if(expr.jjtGetChild(1) instanceof ASTUnaryExpression) {
                                ASTUnaryExpression rightExpr = (ASTUnaryExpression) expr.jjtGetChild(1);
                                if(rightExpr.jjtGetChild(0).getImage().equals(expr.jjtGetChild(0).getImage())) { // check for same variable on both sides
                                    addViolation(data, node);
                                }
                            }
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

==========5轮中每一轮为第一个测试用例生成的checker===============
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.errorprone;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class BrokenNullCheckRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public BrokenNullCheckRule() {
        super(ASTIfStatement.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTIfStatement node, Object data) {
        if (node.jjtGetChild(0) instanceof ASTInfixExpression) {
            ASTInfixExpression expr = (ASTInfixExpression) node.jjtGetChild(0);
            if (expr.hasDescendantOfType(ASTNullLiteral.class)) {
                Node nullCheck = expr.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTNullLiteral.class).jjtGetParent();
                if (nullCheck.jjtGetChild(1) instanceof ASTUnaryExpression) {
                    addViolation(data, node);
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

==========5轮中每一轮为第一个测试用例生成的checker===============
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.errorprone;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class BrokenNullCheckRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public BrokenNullCheckRule() {
        super(ASTInfixExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTInfixExpression node, Object data) {
        if (node.hasDescendantOfType(ASTUnaryExpression.class)) {
            ASTUnaryExpression unaryExpression = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTUnaryExpression.class);
            if (unaryExpression.hasDescendantOfType(ASTMethodCall.class)) {
                ASTMethodCall methodCall = unaryExpression.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTMethodCall.class);
                if (methodCall.hasImageEqualTo("equals")) {
                    addViolation(data, node);
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

================修复新加测试用例后生成的checker===================
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.errorprone;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class BrokenNullCheckRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public BrokenNullCheckRule() {
        super(ASTInfixExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTInfixExpression node, Object data) {
        if (node.hasDescendantOfType(ASTUnaryExpression.class)) {
            ASTUnaryExpression unaryExpression = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTUnaryExpression.class);
            if (unaryExpression.hasDescendantOfType(ASTMethodCall.class)) {
                ASTMethodCall methodCall = unaryExpression.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTMethodCall.class);
                if (methodCall.hasImageEqualTo("equals")) {
                    if (node.getImage().equals("||")) {
                        addViolation(data, node);
                    }
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}
编译是否通过？
True

```
    public BrokenNullCheckRule() {
        super(ASTInfixExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTInfixExpression node, Object data) {

            ASTUnaryExpression unaryExpression = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTUnaryExpression.class);
```

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.errorprone;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class BrokenNullCheckRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public BrokenNullCheckRule() {
        super(ASTInfixExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTInfixExpression node, Object data) {
        if ("||".equals(node.getImage())) {
            for (int i = 0; i < node.jjtGetNumChildren(); i++) {
                Node child = node.jjtGetChild(i);
                if (child instanceof ASTUnaryExpression && child.hasDescendantOfType(ASTMethodCall.class)) {
                    ASTMethodCall methodCall = child.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTMethodCall.class);
                    if ("equals".equals(methodCall.getImage())) {
                        addViolation(data, node);
                    }
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

```
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.errorprone;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class BrokenNullCheckRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public BrokenNullCheckRule() {
        super(ASTInfixExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTInfixExpression node, Object data) {
        if (node.hasDescendantOfType(ASTUnaryExpression.class)) {
            ASTUnaryExpression unaryExpression = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTUnaryExpression.class);
            if (unaryExpression.hasDescendantOfType(ASTMethodCall.class)) {
                ASTMethodCall methodCall = unaryExpression.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTMethodCall.class);
                if (methodCall.hasImageEqualTo("equals")) {
                    addViolation(data, node);
                }
            }
```
        } else if (node.hasDescendantOfType(ASTMethodCall.class)) {

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.errorprone;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class BrokenNullCheckRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public BrokenNullCheckRule() {
        super(ASTInfixExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTInfixExpression node, Object data) {
        Node parent = node.jjtGetParent();
        if(parent instanceof ASTExpression && node.hasDescendantOfType(ASTMethodCall.class)) {
            ASTMethodCall methodCall = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTMethodCall.class);
            if (methodCall.hasImageEqualTo("equals")) {
                ASTInfixExpression infixExpression = (ASTInfixExpression) parent.jjtGetChild(0);
                if (infixExpression.isAnd() || (infixExpression.isOr() && infixExpression.jjtGetChildIndex() > 0)) {
                    addViolation(data, node);
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.errorprone;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class BrokenNullCheckRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public BrokenNullCheckRule() {
        super(ASTInfixExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTInfixExpression node, Object data) {
        if ((node.isOr() && node.hasDescendantOfType(ASTMethodCall.class, 0))
                || (node.isAnd() && node.hasDescendantOfType(ASTMethodCall.class, 1))) {
            
            ASTMethodCall methodCall = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTMethodCall.class);
            if (methodCall.hasImageEqualTo("equals")) {
                addViolation(data, node);
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.errorprone;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class BrokenNullCheckRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public BrokenNullCheckRule() {
        super(ASTInfixExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTInfixExpression node, Object data) {
        if (node.hasDescendantOfType(ASTUnaryExpression.class)) {
            ASTUnaryExpression unaryExpression = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTUnaryExpression.class);
            if (unaryExpression.hasDescendantOfType(ASTMethodCall.class)) {
                ASTMethodCall methodCall = unaryExpression.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTMethodCall.class);
                if (methodCall.hasImageEqualTo("equals") && node.getImage().equals("&&")) {
                    addViolation(data, node);
                }
            }
        } else if (node.hasDescendantOfType(ASTMethodCall.class)) {
            ASTMethodCall methodCall = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTMethodCall.class);
            if (methodCall.hasImageEqualTo("equals") && node.getImage().equals("||")) {
                if (node.jjtGetChild(0).jjtGetChild(0) instanceof ASTNullLiteral) {
                    addViolation(data, node);
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.errorprone;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class BrokenNullCheckRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public BrokenNullCheckRule() {
        super(ASTInfixExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTInfixExpression node, Object data) {
        if ("&&".equals(node.getOperator())) {
            if (node.hasDescendantOfType(ASTUnaryExpression.class)) {
                ASTUnaryExpression unaryExpression = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTUnaryExpression.class);
                if (unaryExpression.hasDescendantOfType(ASTMethodCall.class)) {
                    ASTMethodCall methodCall = unaryExpression.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTMethodCall.class);
                    if ("equals".equals(methodCall.getName())) {
                        addViolation(data, node);
                    }
                }
            } else if (node.hasDescendantOfType(ASTMethodCall.class)) {
                ASTMethodCall methodCall = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTMethodCall.class);
                if ("equals".equals(methodCall.getName())) {
                    addViolation(data, node);
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.errorprone;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class BrokenNullCheckRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public BrokenNullCheckRule() {
        super(ASTInfixExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTInfixExpression node, Object data) {
        if (node.isOr()) {
            Node left = node.jjtGetChild(0);
            Node right = node.jjtGetChild(1);
            if (left instanceof ASTEqualityExpression && right instanceof ASTMethodCall) {
                ASTEqualityExpression equalityExpression = (ASTEqualityExpression) left;
                ASTMethodCall methodCall = (ASTMethodCall) right;
                if (isEqualNullCheck(equalityExpression) && isEqualsMethodCall(methodCall)) {
                    addViolation(data, node);
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    private boolean isEqualNullCheck(ASTEqualityExpression equalityExpression) {
        return equalityExpression.isEqual() && equalityExpression.jjtGetChild(1) instanceof ASTNullLiteral;
    }

    private boolean isEqualsMethodCall(ASTMethodCall methodCall) {
        return "equals".equals(methodCall.getMethodName());
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.errorprone;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class BrokenNullCheckRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public BrokenNullCheckRule() {
        super(ASTConditionalAndExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTConditionalAndExpression node, Object data) {
        ASTPrimaryExpression left = node.jjtGetChild(0).getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTPrimaryExpression.class);
        ASTPrimaryExpression right = node.jjtGetChild(1).getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTPrimaryExpression.class);

        if (left == null || right == null) {
            return super.visit(node, data);
        }

        ASTPrimaryPrefix leftPrefix = left.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTPrimaryPrefix.class);
        ASTPrimaryPrefix rightPrefix = right.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTPrimaryPrefix.class);

        if (leftPrefix == null || rightPrefix == null) {
            return super.visit(node, data);
        }

        ASTName leftName = leftPrefix.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTName.class);
        ASTName rightName = rightPrefix.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTName.class);

        if (leftName == null || rightName == null) {
            return super.visit(node, data);
        }

        if (leftName.hasImageEqualTo(rightName.getImage()) && left.jjtGetChild(1) instanceof ASTPrimarySuffix && right.jjtGetChild(1) instanceof ASTPrimarySuffix) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }

        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

```
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;

public class BrokenNullCheckRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public BrokenNullCheckRule() {
        super(ASTInfixExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTInfixExpression node, Object data) {
        if (node.hasDescendantOfType(ASTUnaryExpression.class)) {
            ASTUnaryExpression unaryExpression = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTUnaryExpression.class);
            if (unaryExpression.hasDescendantOfType(ASTMethodCall.class)) {
                ASTMethodCall methodCall = unaryExpression.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTMethodCall.class);
                if (methodCall.hasImageEqualTo("equals")) {
                    addViolation(data, node);
                }

                addViolation(data, node);
```

You have helped me write a checker for this rule:
Rule description: The null check is broken since it will throw a NullPointerException itself. It is likely that you used || instead of && or vice versa.;
And the source code of the checker is as follows:
```
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.errorprone;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class BrokenNullCheckRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public BrokenNullCheckRule() {
        super(ASTInfixExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTInfixExpression node, Object data) {
        if (node.hasDescendantOfType(ASTUnaryExpression.class)) {
            ASTUnaryExpression unaryExpression = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTUnaryExpression.class);
            if (unaryExpression.hasDescendantOfType(ASTMethodCall.class)) {
                ASTMethodCall methodCall = unaryExpression.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTMethodCall.class);
                if (methodCall.hasImageEqualTo("equals")) {
                    addViolation(data, node);
                }
            }
        } else if (node.hasDescendantOfType(ASTMethodCall.class)) {
            ASTMethodCall methodCall = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTMethodCall.class);
            if (methodCall.hasImageEqualTo("equals")) {
                addViolation(data, node);
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}
```

This checker has passed this negative testcase:
public class Foo {
    Object buz;
    Object bar(Object list) {
        if (list != null || !list.equals(buz)) {
            return list;
        }
    }
}
This checker has passed this negative testcase:
public class Foo {
    Object buz;
    Object bar(Object list) {
        if (list == null && list.equals(buz)) {
            return list;
        }
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.errorprone;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class BrokenNullCheckRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public BrokenNullCheckRule() {
        super(ASTInfixExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTInfixExpression node, Object data) {
        if (node.hasDescendantOfType(ASTUnaryExpression.class)) {
            ASTUnaryExpression unaryExpression = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTUnaryExpression.class);
            if (unaryExpression.hasDescendantOfType(ASTMethodCall.class)) {
                ASTMethodCall methodCall = unaryExpression.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTMethodCall.class);
                if (methodCall.hasImageEqualTo("equals") || methodCall.hasImageEqualTo("length")) {
                    addViolation(data, node);
                }
            }
        } else if (node.hasDescendantOfType(ASTMethodCall.class)) {
            ASTMethodCall methodCall = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTMethodCall.class);
            if (methodCall.hasImageEqualTo("equals") || methodCall.hasImageEqualTo("length")) {
                addViolation(data, node);
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.errorprone;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class BrokenNullCheckRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public BrokenNullCheckRule() {
        super(ASTInfixExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTInfixExpression node, Object data) {
        if (node.hasDescendantOfType(ASTNullLiteral.class)) {
            if (node.hasDescendantOfType(ASTMethodCall.class)) {
                ASTMethodCall methodCall = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTMethodCall.class);
                if (methodCall.hasImageEqualTo("equals")) {
                    addViolation(data, node);
                }
            } else if (isBooleanComparison(node)) {
                addViolation(data, node);
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    private boolean isBooleanComparison(ASTInfixExpression node) {
        String image = node.getImage();
        return "&&".equals(image) || "||".equals(image);
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.errorprone;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class BrokenNullCheckRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public BrokenNullCheckRule() {
        super(ASTInfixExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTInfixExpression node, Object data) {
        if (node.hasDescendantOfType(ASTUnaryExpression.class)) {
            ASTUnaryExpression unaryExpression = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTUnaryExpression.class);
            if (unaryExpression.hasDescendantOfType(ASTMethodCall.class)) {
                ASTMethodCall methodCall = unaryExpression.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTMethodCall.class);
                if (methodCall.hasImageEqualTo("equals")) {
                    addViolation(data, node);
                }
            }
        } else if (node.hasDescendantOfType(ASTMethodCall.class)) {
            ASTMethodCall methodCall = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTMethodCall.class);
            if (methodCall.hasImageEqualTo("equals")) {
                addViolation(data, node);
            }
        } else if (node.getOperator().equals("&&")) {
            boolean isNullCheck = node.getLhs().hasDescendantOfType(ASTNullLiteral.class);
            boolean isVariableReference = node.getRhs().hasDescendantOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class);
            if (isNullCheck && isVariableReference) {
                addViolation(data, node);
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.errorprone;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class BrokenNullCheckRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public BrokenNullCheckRule() {
        super(ASTInfixExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTInfixExpression node, Object data) {
        if (node.hasDescendantOfType(ASTUnaryExpression.class)) {
            ASTUnaryExpression unaryExpression = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTUnaryExpression.class);
            if (unaryExpression.hasDescendantOfType(ASTMethodCall.class)) {
                ASTMethodCall methodCall = unaryExpression.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTMethodCall.class);
                if (methodCall.hasImageEqualTo("equals")) {
                    addViolation(data, node);
                }
            }
        } else if (node.hasDescendantOfType(ASTMethodCall.class)) {
            ASTMethodCall methodCall = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTMethodCall.class);
            if (methodCall.hasImageEqualTo("equals")) {
                addViolation(data, node);
            }
        } else if (node.hasImageEqualTo("&&") || node.hasImageEqualTo("||")) {
            ASTInfixExpression firstChild = (ASTInfixExpression) node.jjtGetChild(0);
            ASTInfixExpression secondChild = (ASTInfixExpression) node.jjtGetChild(1);
            if (firstChild.hasImageEqualTo("==") && secondChild.hasImageEqualTo("!=")) {
                addViolation(data, node);
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.errorprone;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class BrokenNullCheckRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public BrokenNullCheckRule() {
        super(ASTInfixExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTInfixExpression node, Object data) {
        if (node.hasDescendantOfType(ASTUnaryExpression.class)) {
            ASTUnaryExpression unaryExpression = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTUnaryExpression.class);
            if (unaryExpression.hasDescendantOfType(ASTMethodCall.class)) {
                ASTMethodCall methodCall = unaryExpression.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTMethodCall.class);
                if (methodCall.hasImageEqualTo("equals")) {
                    addViolation(data, node);
                }
            }
        } else if (node.hasDescendantOfType(ASTMethodCall.class)) {
            ASTMethodCall methodCall = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTMethodCall.class);
            if (methodCall.hasImageEqualTo("equals")) {
                addViolation(data, node);
            }
        } else if (node.hasDescendantOfType(ASTInfixExpression.class)) {
            for (ASTInfixExpression infixExpression : node.findDescendantsOfType(ASTInfixExpression.class)) {
                if (infixExpression.getImage().equals("&&") || infixExpression.getImage().equals("||")) {
                    if ((infixExpression.getLeftHandSide().hasDescendantOfType(ASTNullLiteral)) &&
                        (infixExpression.getRightHandSide().hasDescendantOfType(ASTBooleanLiteral))) {
                        addViolation(data, node);
                    }
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.errorprone;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class BrokenNullCheckRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public BrokenNullCheckRule() {
        super();
        addRuleChainVisit(ASTInfixExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTInfixExpression node, Object data) {
        if (node.hasDescendantOfType(ASTUnaryExpression.class)) {
            ASTUnaryExpression unaryExpression = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTUnaryExpression.class);
            if (unaryExpression.hasDescendantOfType(ASTMethodCall.class)) {
                ASTMethodCall methodCall = unaryExpression.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTMethodCall.class);
                if ("equals".equals(methodCall.getImage())) {
                    addViolation(data, node);
                }
            }
        } else if (node.hasDescendantOfType(ASTMethodCall.class)) {
            ASTMethodCall methodCall = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTMethodCall.class);
            if ("equals".equals(methodCall.getImage())) {
                addViolation(data, node);
            }
        } else if (node.hasDescendantOfType(ASTNullLiteral.class)) {
            ASTNullLiteral nullLiteral = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTNullLiteral.class);
            if (nullLiteral.jjtGetParent() instanceof ASTInfixExpression) {
                addViolation(data, node);
            }
        }

        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.errorprone;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class BrokenNullCheckRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public BrokenNullCheckRule() {
        super(ASTInfixExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTInfixExpression node, Object data) {
        if (node.hasDescendantOfType(ASTUnaryExpression.class)) {
            ASTUnaryExpression unaryExpression = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTUnaryExpression.class);
            if (unaryExpression.hasDescendantOfType(ASTMethodCall.class)) {
                ASTMethodCall methodCall = unaryExpression.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTMethodCall.class);
                if (methodCall.hasImageEqualTo("equals")) {
                    addViolation(data, node);
                }
            }
        } else if (node.hasDescendantOfType(ASTMethodCall.class)) {
            ASTMethodCall methodCall = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTMethodCall.class);
            if (methodCall.hasImageEqualTo("equals")) {
                addViolation(data, node);
            }
        } else if (node.hasDescendantOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class)) {
            ASTVariableAccess variableAccess = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class);
            if (variableAccess.hasImageEqualTo("null")) {
                ASTInfixExpression siblingNode = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTInfixExpression.class);
                if (siblingNode != null && siblingNode.hasDescendantOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class)) {
                    addViolation(data, node);
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.errorprone;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class BrokenNullCheckRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public BrokenNullCheckRule() {
        super(ASTInfixExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTInfixExpression node, Object data) {
        ASTExpression firstExpression = node.getFirstChildOfType(ASTExpression.class);
        if (firstExpression != null) {
            checkNullCheck(firstExpression, data);
        }
        ASTExpression secondExpression = node.getSecondChildOfType(ASTExpression.class);
        if (secondExpression != null) {
            checkNullCheck(secondExpression, data);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    private void checkNullCheck(ASTExpression expression, Object data) {
        if (expression.jjtGetNumChildren() > 1 && expression.jjtGetChild(1) instanceof ASTInfixExpression) {
            ASTInfixExpression infixExpression = (ASTInfixExpression) expression.jjtGetChild(1);
            if (infixExpression.getImage().equals("||")) {
                Node firstChild = infixExpression.jjtGetChild(0);
                Node secondChild = infixExpression.jjtGetChild(1);
                if ((firstChild.getImage().equals("null") && !secondChild.getImage().equals("null"))
                        || (!firstChild.getImage().equals("null") && secondChild.getImage().equals("null"))) {
                    addViolation(data, expression);
                }
            }
        }
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.errorprone;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class BrokenNullCheckRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public BrokenNullCheckRule() {
        super(ASTInfixExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTInfixExpression node, Object data) {
        if (node.hasDescendantOfType(ASTUnaryExpression.class)) {
            ASTUnaryExpression unaryExpression = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTUnaryExpression.class);
            if (unaryExpression.hasDescendantOfType(ASTMethodCall.class)) {
                ASTMethodCall methodCall = unaryExpression.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTMethodCall.class);
                if (methodCall.hasImageEqualTo("equals")) {
                    addViolation(data, node);
                }
            }
        } else if (node.hasDescendantOfType(ASTMethodCall.class)) {
            ASTMethodCall methodCall = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTMethodCall.class);
            if (methodCall.hasImageEqualTo("equals")) {
                addViolation(data, node);
            }
        } else if (node.isOr() && node.jjtGetChild(0).hasDescendantOfType(ASTNullLiteral.class) && node.jjtGetChild(1).hasDescendantOfType(ASTInfixExpression.class)) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.errorprone;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class BrokenNullCheckRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public BrokenNullCheckRule() {
        super(ASTInfixExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTInfixExpression node, Object data) {
        if (node.isKind("&&") || node.isKind("||")) {
            AbstractJavaNode firstOperand = (AbstractJavaNode) node.jjtGetChild(0);
            AbstractJavaNode secondOperand = (AbstractJavaNode) node.jjtGetChild(1);
            if (firstOperand instanceof ASTInfixExpression) {
                ASTInfixExpression firstInfixExpression = (ASTInfixExpression) firstOperand;
                if (firstInfixExpression.isKind("!=") && firstInfixExpression.jjtGetChild(1) instanceof ASTNullLiteral) {
                    String varName = ((ASTVariableAccess) firstInfixExpression.jjtGetChild(0)).getImage();
                    if (secondOperand.hasDescendantMatchingXPath(".//ASTVariableAccess[@Image='" + varName + "']")) {
                        addViolation(data, node);
                    }
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.errorprone;



import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class BrokenNullCheckRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public BrokenNullCheckRule() {
        super(ASTInfixExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTInfixExpression node, Object data) {
        if (node.hasDescendantOfType(ASTUnaryExpression.class)) {
            ASTUnaryExpression unaryExpression = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTUnaryExpression.class);
            if (unaryExpression.hasDescendantOfType(ASTMethodCall.class)) {
                ASTMethodCall methodCall = unaryExpression.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTMethodCall.class);
                if (methodCall.hasImageEqualTo("equals")) {
                    addViolation(data, node);
                }
            }
        } else if (node.hasDescendantOfType(ASTMethodCall.class)) {
            ASTMethodCall methodCall = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTMethodCall.class);
            if (methodCall.hasImageEqualTo("equals")) {
                addViolation(data, node);
            }
        } else if (node.jjtGetParent() instanceof ASTAssignmentExpression) {
            ASTAssignmentExpression parent = (ASTAssignmentExpression) node.jjtGetParent();
            if (parent.hasDescendantOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class)) {
                ASTVariableAccess variableAccess = parent.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class);
                if (variableAccess.getType() == Boolean.class && "&&".equals(node.getImage())) {
                    addViolation(data, node);
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.errorprone;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class BrokenNullCheckRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public BrokenNullCheckRule() {
        super(ASTInfixExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTInfixExpression node, Object data) {
        checkNullCheck(node, data);
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    private void checkNullCheck(ASTInfixExpression node, Object data) {
        if (node.hasDescendantOfType(ASTUnaryExpression.class)) {
            ASTUnaryExpression unaryExpression = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTUnaryExpression.class);
            if (unaryExpression.hasDescendantOfType(ASTMethodCall.class)) {
                ASTMethodCall methodCall = unaryExpression.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTMethodCall.class);
                if (methodCall.hasImageEqualTo("equals")) {
                    addViolation(data, node);
                }
            }
        } else if (node.hasDescendantOfType(ASTMethodCall.class)) {
            ASTMethodCall methodCall = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTMethodCall.class);
            if (methodCall.hasImageEqualTo("equals")) {
                addViolation(data, node);
            }
        } else if (node.hasDescendantOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class)) {
            ASTVariableAccess variableAccess = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class);
            if (variableAccess != null) {
                addViolation(data, node);
            }
        }
    }

}

```
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.errorprone;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class BrokenNullCheckRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public BrokenNullCheckRule() {
        super(ASTInfixExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTInfixExpression node, Object data) {
        if (node.hasDescendantOfType(ASTUnaryExpression.class)) {
            ASTUnaryExpression unaryExpression = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTUnaryExpression.class);
            if (unaryExpression.hasDescendantOfType(ASTMethodCall.class)) {
                addViolation(data, node);
            }
        } else if (node.hasDescendantOfType(ASTMethodCall.class)) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}
```

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.errorprone;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class BrokenNullCheckRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public BrokenNullCheckRule() {
        addRuleChainVisit(ASTInfixExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTInfixExpression node, Object data) {
        if (node.hasDescendantOfType(ASTUnaryExpression.class)) {
            ASTUnaryExpression unaryExpression = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTUnaryExpression.class);
            if (unaryExpression.hasDescendantOfType(ASTMethodCall.class)) {
                ASTMethodCall methodCall = unaryExpression.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTMethodCall.class);
                if (methodCall.hasImageEqualTo("equals")) {
                    addViolation(data, node);
                }
            }
        } else if (node.hasDescendantOfType(ASTMethodCall.class)) {
            ASTMethodCall methodCall = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTMethodCall.class);
            if (methodCall.hasImageEqualTo("equals")) {
                addViolation(data, node);
            }
        } else if (node.hasDescendantOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class)) {
            ASTVariableAccess variableAccess = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class);
            if (variableAccess.getImage().equals("null") && node.hasDescendantMatchingXPath(
                    "./PrimaryExpression/PrimaryPrefix/Name[ends-with(@Image, 'toString') or ends-with(@Image, 'hashCode') or contains(@Image, 'field') or contains(@Image, 'new')]")) {
                addViolation(data, node);
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.errorprone;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class BrokenNullCheckRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public BrokenNullCheckRule() {
        super(ASTInfixExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTInfixExpression node, Object data) {
        if (node.hasDescendantOfType(ASTUnaryExpression.class)) {
            ASTUnaryExpression unaryExpression = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTUnaryExpression.class);
            if (unaryExpression.hasDescendantOfType(ASTMethodCall.class)) {
                ASTMethodCall methodCall = unaryExpression.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTMethodCall.class);
                if (methodCall.hasImageEqualTo("equals")) {
                    addViolation(data, node);
                }
            }
        } else if (node.hasDescendantOfType(ASTMethodCall.class)) {
            ASTMethodCall methodCall = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTMethodCall.class);
            if (methodCall.hasImageEqualTo("equals")) {
                addViolation(data, node);
            }
        } else {
            for (int i = 0; i < node.jjtGetNumChildren(); i++) {
                if (node.jjtGetChild(i) instanceof ASTExpression) {
                    ASTExpression expression = (ASTExpression) node.jjtGetChild(i);
                    if (expression.hasDescendantOfType(ASTInfixExpression.class)) {
                        ASTInfixExpression infixExpression = expression.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTInfixExpression.class);
                        if (infixExpression.hasImageEqualTo("&&") && infixExpression.jjtGetChild(0).hasImageEqualTo("null")) {
                            addViolation(data, node);
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class BrokenNullCheckRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public BrokenNullCheckRule() {
        super(ASTInfixExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTInfixExpression node, Object data) {
        if (node.hasDescendantOfType(ASTUnaryExpression.class)) {
            ASTUnaryExpression unaryExpression = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTUnaryExpression.class);
            if (unaryExpression.hasDescendantOfType(ASTMethodCall.class)) {
                ASTMethodCall methodCall = unaryExpression.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTMethodCall.class);
                if (methodCall.hasImageEqualTo("equals")) {
                    addViolation(data, node);
                }
            }
        } else if (node.hasDescendantOfType(ASTMethodCall.class)) {
            ASTMethodCall methodCall = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTMethodCall.class);
            if (methodCall.hasImageEqualTo("equals")) {
                addViolation(data, node);
            }
        } else if (node.hasDescendantOfType(ASTMethodReference.class)) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        } else if (node.hasDescendantOfType(ASTFieldAccess.class)) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        } else if (node.hasDescendantOfType(ASTConstructorCall.class)) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.errorprone;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class BrokenNullCheckRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public BrokenNullCheckRule() {
        super(ASTInfixExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTInfixExpression node, Object data) {
        if (node.hasDescendantOfType(ASTUnaryExpression.class)) {
            ASTUnaryExpression unaryExpression = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTUnaryExpression.class);
            if (unaryExpression.hasDescendantOfType(ASTMethodCall.class) || unaryExpression.hasDescendantOfType(ASTFieldAccess.class)) {
                addViolation(data, unaryExpression);
            }
        } else if (node.hasDescendantOfType(ASTMethodCall.class) || node.hasDescendantOfType(ASTFieldAccess.class)) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.errorprone;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class BrokenNullCheckRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public BrokenNullCheckRule() {
        super(ASTInfixExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTInfixExpression node, Object data) {
        if (node.hasDescendantOfType(ASTUnaryExpression.class)) {
            ASTUnaryExpression unaryExpression = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTUnaryExpression.class);
            if (unaryExpression.hasDescendantOfType(ASTMethodCall.class)) {
                ASTMethodCall methodCall = unaryExpression.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTMethodCall.class);
                if (methodCall.hasImageEqualTo("equals")) {
                    addViolation(data, node);
                }
            }
        } else if (node.hasDescendantOfType(ASTMethodCall.class)) {
            ASTMethodCall methodCall = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTMethodCall.class);
            if (methodCall.hasImageEqualTo("equals")) {
                addViolation(data, node);
            }
        }
        // Add check for array access after null check
        else if (node.hasDescendantOfType(ASTArrayAccess.class)) {
            ASTArrayAccess arrayAccess = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTArrayAccess.class);
            if (node.hasImageEqualTo("null") && arrayAccess.jjtGetParent() instanceof ASTInfixExpression) {
                addViolation(data, node);
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.errorprone;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class BrokenNullCheckRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public BrokenNullCheckRule() {
        super();
        addRuleChainVisit(ASTInfixExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTInfixExpression node, Object data) {
        if (node.hasDescendantOfType(ASTUnaryExpression.class)) {
            ASTUnaryExpression unaryExpression = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTUnaryExpression.class);
            if (unaryExpression.hasDescendantOfType(ASTMethodCall.class)) {
                ASTMethodCall methodCall = unaryExpression.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTMethodCall.class);
                if ("equals".equals(methodCall.getImage())) {
                    addViolation(data, node);
                }
            }
        } else if (node.hasDescendantOfType(ASTMethodCall.class)) {
            ASTMethodCall methodCall = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTMethodCall.class);
            if ("equals".equals(methodCall.getImage())) {
                addViolation(data, node);
            }
        } else if (node.hasDescendantOfType(ASTArrayAccess.class)) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return data;
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.errorprone;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class BrokenNullCheckRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public BrokenNullCheckRule() {
        super(ASTInfixExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTInfixExpression node, Object data) {
        if (node.hasDescendantOfType(ASTUnaryExpression.class)) {
            ASTUnaryExpression unaryExpression = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTUnaryExpression.class);
            if (unaryExpression.hasDescendantOfType(ASTMethodCall.class)) {
                ASTMethodCall methodCall = unaryExpression.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTMethodCall.class);
                if (methodCall.hasImageEqualTo("equals")) {
                    addViolation(data, node);
                }
            }
        } else if (node.hasDescendantOfType(ASTMethodCall.class)) {
            ASTMethodCall methodCall = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTMethodCall.class);
            if (methodCall.hasImageEqualTo("equals")) {
                addViolation(data, node);
            }
        } else if (node.hasDescendantOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class)) {
            ASTVariableAccess variableAccess = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class);
            if (variableAccess.hasImageEqualTo("null") && node.getSecondChild().isFindBoundary()) {
                addViolation(data, node);
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.errorprone;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class BrokenNullCheckRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public BrokenNullCheckRule() {
        super(ASTInfixExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTInfixExpression node, Object data) {
        if ("&&".equals(node.getImage())) {
            for (int i = 0; i < node.getNumChildren(); i++) {
                Node child = node.getChild(i);
                if (child instanceof ASTNullLiteral) {
                    Node sibling = getSibling(node, i);
                    if (sibling instanceof ASTInfixExpression) {
                        checkInfixExpression((ASTInfixExpression) sibling, data);
                    }
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    private void checkInfixExpression(ASTInfixExpression node, Object data) {
        for (int i = 0; i < node.getNumChildren(); i++) {
            Node child = node.getChild(i);
            if (child instanceof ASTVariableAccess) {
                addViolation(data, node);
            }
        }
    }

    private Node getSibling(Node node, int index) {
        if (index == node.getNumChildren() - 1) {
            return node.getChild(index - 1);
        } else {
            return node.getChild(index + 1);
        }
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.errorprone;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class BrokenNullCheckRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public BrokenNullCheckRule() {
        super(ASTInfixExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTInfixExpression node, Object data) {
        if (node.hasDescendantOfType(ASTUnaryExpression.class)) {
            ASTUnaryExpression unaryExpression = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTUnaryExpression.class);
            if (unaryExpression.hasDescendantOfType(ASTMethodCall.class)) {
                ASTMethodCall methodCall = unaryExpression.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTMethodCall.class);
                if (methodCall.hasImageEqualTo("equals")) {
                    addViolation(data, node);
                }
            }
        } else if (node.hasDescendantOfType(ASTMethodCall.class)) {
            ASTMethodCall methodCall = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTMethodCall.class);
            if (methodCall.hasImageEqualTo("equals")) {
                addViolation(data, node);
            }
        } else if (node.hasDescendantOfType(ASTInfixExpression.class)) {
            ASTInfixExpression infixExpression = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTInfixExpression.class);
            if (infixExpression.hasDescendantOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class) && 
                infixExpression.hasDescendantOfType(ASTNumericLiteral.class)) {
                addViolation(data, node);
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class BrokenNullCheckRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public BrokenNullCheckRule() {
        super(ASTInfixExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTInfixExpression node, Object data) {
        if (node.hasDescendantOfType(ASTUnaryExpression.class)) {
            ASTUnaryExpression unaryExpression = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTUnaryExpression.class);
            if (unaryExpression.hasDescendantOfType(ASTMethodCall.class)) {
                ASTMethodCall methodCall = unaryExpression.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTMethodCall.class);
                if (methodCall.hasImageEqualTo("equals") && isNullCheck(node)) {
                    addViolation(data, node);
                }
            }
        } else if (node.hasDescendantOfType(ASTMethodCall.class)) {
            ASTMethodCall methodCall = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTMethodCall.class);
            if (methodCall.hasImageEqualTo("equals") && isNullCheck(node)) {
                addViolation(data, node);
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    private boolean isNullCheck(ASTInfixExpression node) {
        return node.hasDescendantOfType(ASTNullLiteral.class) 
            && (node.hasImageEqualTo("||") || node.hasImageEqualTo("&&"));
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.errorprone;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class BrokenNullCheckRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTIfStatement node, Object data) {
        ASTExpression expression = (ASTExpression) node.jjtGetChild(0);
        checkInfixExpression(expression, data);
        return data;
    }

    private void checkInfixExpression(AbstractJavaNode node, Object data) {
        for (int i = 0; i < node.jjtGetNumChildren(); i++) {
            AbstractJavaNode child = (AbstractJavaNode) node.jjtGetChild(i);
            if (child instanceof ASTInfixExpression) {
                ASTInfixExpression infixExpression = (ASTInfixExpression) child;
                if (infixExpression.hasImageEqualTo("||") || infixExpression.hasImageEqualTo("&&")) {
                    checkNullCheckAndEqualsCall(infixExpression, data);
                }
                checkInfixExpression(child, data);
            }
        }
    }

    private void checkNullCheckAndEqualsCall(ASTInfixExpression infixExpression, Object data) {
        for (int i = 0; i < infixExpression.jjtGetNumChildren(); i++) {
            AbstractJavaNode child = (AbstractJavaNode) infixExpression.jjtGetChild(i);
            if (child instanceof ASTPrimaryExpression) {
                ASTPrimaryExpression primaryExpression = (ASTPrimaryExpression) child;
                ASTPrimaryPrefix prefix = (ASTPrimaryPrefix) primaryExpression.jjtGetChild(0);
                if (prefix.jjtGetNumChildren() > 0 && prefix.jjtGetChild(0) instanceof ASTPrimarySuffix) {
                    ASTPrimarySuffix suffix = (ASTPrimarySuffix) prefix.jjtGetChild(0);
                    if (suffix.hasImageEqualTo("equals") && !isNullCheckedBefore(infixExpression, primaryExpression)) {
                        addViolation(data, infixExpression);
                    }
                }
            }
        }
    }

    private boolean isNullCheckedBefore(ASTInfixExpression infixExpression, ASTPrimaryExpression primaryExpression) {
        for (int i = 0; i < infixExpression.jjtGetNumChildren(); i++) {
            AbstractJavaNode child = (AbstractJavaNode) infixExpression.jjtGetChild(i);
            if (child instanceof ASTInfixExpression) {
                ASTInfixExpression childInfixExpression = (ASTInfixExpression) child;
                if (childInfixExpression.hasImageEqualTo("==") || childInfixExpression.hasImageEqualTo("!=")) {
                    for (int j = 0; j < childInfixExpression.jjtGetNumChildren(); j++) {
                        AbstractJavaNode grandchild = (AbstractJavaNode) childInfixExpression.jjtGetChild(j);
                        if (grandchild instanceof ASTPrimaryExpression) {
                            ASTPrimaryExpression grandchildPrimaryExpression = (ASTPrimaryExpression) grandchild;
                            if (grandchildPrimaryExpression.jjtGetChild(0).hasImageEqualTo(primaryExpression.jjtGetChild(0).getImage())) {
                                return true;
                            }
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
        }
        return false;
    }
}

================修复新加测试用例后生成的checker===================
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.errorprone;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class BrokenNullCheckRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public BrokenNullCheckRule() {
        super(ASTInfixExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTInfixExpression node, Object data) {
        if (node.hasDescendantOfType(ASTUnaryExpression.class)) {
            ASTUnaryExpression unaryExpression = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTUnaryExpression.class);
            if (unaryExpression.hasDescendantOfType(ASTMethodCall.class)) {
                ASTMethodCall methodCall = unaryExpression.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTMethodCall.class);
                if (methodCall.hasImageEqualTo("equals") && hasNullCheckForSameVariable(node, methodCall)) {
                    addViolation(data, node);
                }
            }
        } else if (node.hasDescendantOfType(ASTMethodCall.class)) {
            ASTMethodCall methodCall = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTMethodCall.class);
            if (methodCall.hasImageEqualTo("equals") && hasNullCheckForSameVariable(node, methodCall)) {
                addViolation(data, node);
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    private boolean hasNullCheckForSameVariable(ASTInfixExpression node, ASTMethodCall methodCall) {
        if (node.hasDescendantOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class) && methodCall.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class) != null) {
            ASTVariableAccess variable1 = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class);
            ASTVariableAccess variable2 = methodCall.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class);
            return variable1.hasImageEqualTo(variable2.getImage());
        }
        return false;
    }
}

```
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.errorprone;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class BrokenNullCheckRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public BrokenNullCheckRule() {
        super(ASTInfixExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTInfixExpression node, Object data) {
        if (node.hasDescendantOfType(ASTUnaryExpression.class)) {
            ASTUnaryExpression unaryExpression = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTUnaryExpression.class);
            if (unaryExpression.hasDescendantOfType(ASTMethodCall.class)) {
                ASTMethodCall methodCall = unaryExpression.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTMethodCall.class);
                if (methodCall.hasImageEqualTo("equals")) {
                    addViolation(data, node);
                }
            }
        } else if (node.hasDescendantOfType(ASTMethodCall.class)) {
            ASTMethodCall methodCall = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTMethodCall.class);
            if (methodCall.hasImageEqualTo("equals")) {
                addViolation(data, node);
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}
```

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.errorprone;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class BrokenNullCheckRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public BrokenNullCheckRule() {
        super(ASTInfixExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTInfixExpression node, Object data) {
        if (node.hasDescendantOfType(ASTUnaryExpression.class)) {
            ASTUnaryExpression unaryExpression = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTUnaryExpression.class);
            if (unaryExpression.hasDescendantOfType(ASTMethodCall.class)) {
                ASTMethodCall methodCall = unaryExpression.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTMethodCall.class);
                if (methodCall.hasImageEqualTo("equals")) {
                    checkForNullCheck(node, data);
                }
            }
        } else if (node.hasDescendantOfType(ASTMethodCall.class)) {
            ASTMethodCall methodCall = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTMethodCall.class);
            if (methodCall.hasImageEqualTo("equals")) {
                checkForNullCheck(node, data);
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    private void checkForNullCheck(Node node, Object data) {
        Node parent = node.jjtGetParent();
        for (int i = 0; i < parent.jjtGetNumChildren(); i++) {
            Node sibling = parent.jjtGetChild(i);
            if (sibling instanceof ASTInfixExpression && sibling.hasImageEqualTo("==")) {
                Node potentialNullCheck = sibling.getFirstChildOfType(ASTInfixExpression.class);
                if (potentialNullCheck != null && potentialNullCheck.hasImageEqualTo("null")) {
                    addViolation(data, node);
                    break;
                }
            }
        }
    }
}

================修复新加测试用例后生成的checker===================
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.errorprone;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class BrokenNullCheckRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {

    public BrokenNullCheckRule() {
        super(ASTInfixExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTInfixExpression node, Object data) {
        if (node.hasDescendantOfType(ASTNullLiteral.class) && 
            node.hasDescendantOfType(ASTMethodCall.class)) {
            ASTMethodCall methodCall = node.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTMethodCall.class);
            ASTPrimaryExpression primaryExpression = methodCall.getFirstParentOfType(ASTPrimaryExpression.class);

            if (primaryExpression != null) {
                ASTPrimaryPrefix prefix = primaryExpression.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTPrimaryPrefix.class);
                if (prefix != null && prefix.usesThisModifier()) {
                    addViolation(data, node);
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}
